<review>If I could give more than 5 stars I would !!!  This is one of the best Goodwills in the country and it is NEVER PICKED THROUGH !!!  It's insane how there is constantly fresh merchandise coming through here - if you come to the Baldwin Park store at 10 in the morning and look at everything, then you come back at 7 pm that same day, it's like the store grew amazing new designer dresses and brand new power tools right out of the impeccably clean tiled floors !!!  Baldwin Park is a town back on the rise located just slightly west of West Covina and the energy of the staff is so positive even if you didn't buy anything (which is virtually IMPOSSIBLE given that the selection of merchandise is unreal), there is no way you could leave the store without feeling like you are walking on air and in touch with all that is good with the Earth and mankind.  I am a diehard thrift store junkie and have been to every Goodwill in California from Chula Vista all the way north to Weed and after only being open not even three months yet, the Baldwin Park Goodwill is easily in the top five !!! < text>
Simply put: the best Thai massage I have found in Los Angeles CA.  I have been twice, I experienced two different masseuses, and BOTH times I left feeling completely worked over, total body devastation, IN A GOOD WAY!  They turned me into jelly, which my body desperately needed.

On my most recent visit my therapist was fantastic and I am completely comfortable recommending her. She spoke English perfectly, which seems to be not common at these Thai massage businesses, she understands THE LANGUAGE OF THE BODY.  She gave me the pressure I needed and checked in with me to make sure it was okay.  You could tell her hands and feet were experienced and she was responding to the feedback my body was giving her without my having to speak it out loud.  (Which is good, given that I was face down for at least half the time.)

Whatever screening process they use for their staff, whatever school or training academy they are recruiting them from (presumably somewhere in Thailand, but who knows) it's working.

I booked a 90-minute session, which included 30 minutes of foot reflexology, and I have to tell you, probably the best massage in my life.  I went in a ball of tension and I left feeling like a blissed out quivering mound of jelly.< /text>
